# Stored genus-3 ribbon graph data
# How to read this file:
# - Topology N matches the numbering used by get_stored_genus3_graph(N) in genus3_t_duality.py.
# - Each topology here is a one-face ribbon graph.
# - edges = ((edge_label, vertex_a, vertex_b), ...).
# - boundary = ((from_vertex, to_vertex, edge_label), ...) listed counterclockwise
#   around the disc; the tuple position is the boundary segment number, starting at 1.
# - sewing_pairs = ((edge_label, seg1, seg2), ...) means boundary segments seg1 and
#   seg2 are glued with opposite orientation to form edge edge_label.
# - All labels are 1-based integers.
